        chapter) or Rule 12b&#8208;2 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (&#167;240.12b&#8208;2 of this chapter).</div>

    <td style="width: 54pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Item 1.02.</td>

    <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Termination of Material Definitive Agreement.</div>
            </td>

  </tr>


</table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

      <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On October 30, 2025, Core Scientific, Inc., a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Company</span>&#8221; or &#8220;<span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Core Scientific</span>&#8221;), held a special meeting of stockholders (the &#8220;<span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Special Meeting</span>&#8221;) to consider a proposal
        (the &#8220;<span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Merger Agreement Proposal</span>&#8221;) to <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">adopt the Agreement and Plan of Merger (the &#8220;</span><span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Merger Agreement</span><span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">&#8221;), dated as of July 7, 2025, by and among the Company, CoreWeave, Inc., a
          Delaware corporation (&#8220;</span><span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">CoreWeave</span><span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">&#8221;) and Miami Merger Sub I, Inc., a Delaware
          corporation and a wholly owned subsidiary of CoreWeave (&#8220;</span><span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Merger Sub</span><span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">&#8221;), pursuant
          to which and subject to the terms and conditions set forth therein, Merger Sub would merge with and into Core Scientific, with Core Scientific continuing as the surviving company in the merger and as a wholly owned subsidiary of CoreWeave.</span></div>

      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

      <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">At the Special Meeting, the requisite Company stockholders did not approve the Merger
          Agreement Proposal. As a result, on </span><span style="font-size: 10pt;">October 30<span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">, 2025, pursuant to and in accordance with the Merger Agreement, Core Scientific terminated the Merger Agreement,
            effective immediately.</span></span></div>

      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

        Exhibit 99.1.</div>

        density computing, the blockchain industry and the blockchain hosting market; price volatility of digital assets and bitcoin in particular; potential changes in the interpretive positions of the SEC or its staff with respect to digital asset mining
        firms; the likelihood that U.S. federal and state legislatures and regulatory agencies will enact laws and regulations to regulate digital assets and digital asset intermediaries; changing expectations with respect to ESG policies; the
        effectiveness of our compliance and risk management methods; the adequacy of our sources of recovery if the digital assets held by us are lost, stolen or destroyed due to third-party digital asset services; Any such forward-looking statements

      <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Core Scientific Announces Termination of Merger Agreement with CoreWeave</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">AUSTIN, Texas, October 30, 2025 </font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">-</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;"> Core Scientific, Inc</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">. <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">(NASDAQ:
            CORZ)</font> (&#8220;Core Scientific&#8221; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;), a leader in digital infrastructure for high-density colocation services and digital asset mining, previously announced that at a special meeting of Core Scientific stockholders, the Company did
          not receive the votes necessary to approve the previously announced merger agreement with CoreWeave, Inc. (&#8220;CoreWeave&#8221;).&#160; </font></div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><a name="z_Hlk212666640"></a>On October 30, 2025, pursuant to and in accordance with the merger agreement, Core Scientific terminated the merger agreement with CoreWeave,
        effective immediately.&#160; Core Scientific will remain a publicly traded company, and the Company&#8217;s common stock will continue to trade on Nasdaq under the ticker symbol CORZ<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">.</font></div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;"><a name="Section2"></a><a name="Section3"></a>ABOUT CORE SCIENTIFIC</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Core Scientific, Inc. (&#8220;Core Scientific&#8221; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) is a leader in digital
          infrastructure for high-density colocation services and digital asset mining. We operate dedicated, purpose-built facilities for high-density colocation services and are a premier provider of digital infrastructure, software solutions and
          services to our third-party customers. We employ our own fleet of computers (&#8220;miners&#8221;) to earn digital assets for our own account and we are in the process of converting most of our existing facilities to support artificial intelligence-related
          workloads and next generation colocation services. We currently derive the majority of our revenue from earning digital assets for our own account but expect to rapidly increase revenue derived from high-density colocation (&#8220;HDC&#8221;). We currently
          intend to repurpose our remaining facilities currently used in our digital asset mining businesses to support our high-density colocation computing services business as circumstances allow and in a manner designed to retain access to electrical
          power under our control, maximize the value of our digital asset mining equipment to third parties, and fulfill our existing obligations to suppliers and customers. Our facilities are located in Alabama (1), Georgia (2), Kentucky (1), North
          Carolina (1), North Dakota (1), Oklahoma (1) and Texas (3). To learn more, visit </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">www.corescientific.com<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">.</font></font></div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;" class="BRPFPageBreakArea">
        <div style="page-break-after: always;" class="BRPFPageBreak">
          <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
        <div class="BRPFPageHeader" style="width: 100%;">
          <div style="text-align: right; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;"> <img src="image00001.jpg"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">SPECIAL NOTE REGARDING FORWARD-LOOKING STATEMENTS</div>

        cause actual results to differ materially, including: our ability to earn digital assets profitably and to attract customers for our high density colocation capabilities; our ability to perform under our existing colocation agreements, our ability
        to maintain our competitive position in our existing operating segments, the impact of increases in total network hash rate; our ability to raise additional capital to continue our expansion efforts or other operations; our need for significant
        electric power and the limited availability of power resources; the potential failure in our critical systems, facilities or services we provide; the physical risks and regulatory changes relating to climate change; potential significant changes to
        the method of validating blockchain transactions; our vulnerability to physical security breaches, which could disrupt our operations; a potential slowdown in market and economic conditions, particularly those impacting high density computing, the
